local CoreGui = game:GetService("CoreGui")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

local MoonLightHub = {}

if CoreGui:FindFirstChild("MoonLightHub_UI_V9") then
    CoreGui.MoonLightHub_UI_V9:Destroy()
end

function MoonLightHub:CreateWindow(titleText, versionText)
    local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    ScreenGui.Name = "MoonLightHub_UI_V9"
    ScreenGui.Parent = CoreGui
    ScreenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false

    local MainFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 720, 0, 480) 
    MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -360, 0.5, -240)
    MainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 18, 22)
    MainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.18
    MainFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    MainFrame.Parent = ScreenGui

    Instance.new("UICorner", MainFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 12)
    local MainStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", MainFrame)
    MainStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(60, 60, 70)
    MainStroke.Thickness = 1.2

    -- Blur nền
    local Blur = Instance.new("BlurEffect")
    Blur.Size = 16
    Blur.Parent = game:GetService("Lighting")


    local ResizeHandle = Instance.new("TextButton")
    ResizeHandle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
    ResizeHandle.Position = UDim2.new(1, -20, 1, -20)
    ResizeHandle.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    ResizeHandle.Text = ""
    ResizeHandle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 100)
    ResizeHandle.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    ResizeHandle.TextSize = 14
    ResizeHandle.ZIndex = 100 
    ResizeHandle.Parent = MainFrame

    local resizing = false
    local resizeStartPos
    local resizeStartSize

    ResizeHandle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            resizing = true
            resizeStartPos = input.Position
            resizeStartSize = MainFrame.AbsoluteSize
            
            input.Changed:Connect(function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    resizing = false
                end
            end)
        end
    end)

    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            if resizing then
                local delta = input.Position - resizeStartPos
                
                local newWidth = math.clamp(resizeStartSize.X + delta.X, 550, 1500)
                local newHeight = math.clamp(resizeStartSize.Y + delta.Y, 350, 1000)
                
                MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, newWidth, 0, newHeight)
            end
        end
    end)

    local TopBar = Instance.new("Frame")
    TopBar.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
    TopBar.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    TopBar.Parent = MainFrame

    local Title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    Title.Size = UDim2.new(0, 85, 1, 0)
    Title.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 0)
    Title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    Title.Text = titleText or "Moon Light Hub"
    Title.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    Title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    Title.TextSize = 16
    Title.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    Title.Parent = TopBar

    local VerBox = Instance.new("Frame")
    VerBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, 22)
    VerBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, 105, 0.5, -11)
    VerBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 35, 55) 
    VerBox.Parent = TopBar
    Instance.new("UICorner", VerBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
    Instance.new("UIStroke", VerBox).Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 100, 200)

    local VerText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    VerText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    VerText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    VerText.Text = versionText or "v1.0.1 - BETA"
    VerText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 170, 255)
    VerText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    VerText.TextSize = 11
    VerText.Parent = VerBox

    local Arrows = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    Arrows.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 1, 0)
    Arrows.Position = UDim2.new(0, 215, 0, 0)
    Arrows.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    Arrows.RichText = true
    Arrows.Text = [[<font color="#3282F6">>></font> <font color="#3282F6">>></font> <font color="#3282F6">>></font> <font color="#3282F6">>></font> >> >> >> >>]]
    Arrows.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
    Arrows.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    Arrows.TextSize = 16
    Arrows.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    Arrows.Parent = TopBar

    local MinBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    MinBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 30)
    MinBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -75, 0.5, -15) 
    MinBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    MinBtn.Text = "—" 
    MinBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
    MinBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    MinBtn.TextSize = 14
    MinBtn.Parent = TopBar
    MinBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function() TweenService:Create(MinBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play() end)
    MinBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function() TweenService:Create(MinBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)}):Play() end)

    local CloseBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    CloseBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 30)
    CloseBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0.5, -15)
    CloseBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    CloseBtn.Text = "X" 
    CloseBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
    CloseBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    CloseBtn.TextSize = 15
    CloseBtn.Parent = TopBar
    CloseBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function() TweenService:Create(CloseBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 60, 60)}):Play() end)
    CloseBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function() TweenService:Create(CloseBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)}):Play() end)

    -- ── Hàm đóng/mở có animation ──────────────────
    local isOpen = true
    local isTweening = false

    local function OpenMenu()
        if isTweening then return end
        isTweening = true
        MainFrame.Visible = true
        MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
        MainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Blur.Size = 0
        local tw1 = TweenService:Create(MainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.45, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 720, 0, 480),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -360, 0.5, -240),
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.18,
        })
        local tw2 = TweenService:Create(Blur, TweenInfo.new(0.45), {Size = 16})
        tw1:Play(); tw2:Play()
        tw1.Completed:Connect(function() isTweening = false; isOpen = true end)
    end

    local function CloseMenu()
        if isTweening then return end
        isTweening = true
        isOpen = false
        local tw1 = TweenService:Create(MainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
            Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
            Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        })
        local tw2 = TweenService:Create(Blur, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {Size = 0})
        tw1:Play(); tw2:Play()
        tw1.Completed:Connect(function()
            MainFrame.Visible = false
            isTweening = false
        end)
    end

    -- Nút toggle nổi góc màn hình
    local ToggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    ToggleBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 44)
    ToggleBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -22)
    ToggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 18, 22)
    ToggleBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.2
    ToggleBtn.Text = ""
    ToggleBtn.ZIndex = 200
    ToggleBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
    ToggleBtn.Parent = ScreenGui
    Instance.new("UICorner", ToggleBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
    local TBStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", ToggleBtn)
    TBStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
    TBStroke.Thickness = 1.5

    local TBIcon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
    TBIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 26, 0, 26)
    TBIcon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -13, 0.5, -13)
    TBIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    TBIcon.Image = "rbxassetid://10734950309"
    TBIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
    TBIcon.Parent = ToggleBtn

    ToggleBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(ToggleBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
        TweenService:Create(TBIcon, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
    end)
    ToggleBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        TweenService:Create(ToggleBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.2}):Play()
        TweenService:Create(TBIcon, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)}):Play()
    end)
    ToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if isOpen then CloseMenu() else OpenMenu() end
    end)

    -- Mở menu lần đầu có animation
    MainFrame.Visible = false
    OpenMenu()

    CloseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() ScreenGui:Destroy(); Blur:Destroy() end)
    MinBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() CloseMenu() end)

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if not gameProcessed and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.RightControl then
            if isOpen then CloseMenu() else OpenMenu() end
        end
    end)

    local dragging, dragInput, dragStart, startPos
    TopBar.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true; dragStart = input.Position; startPos = MainFrame.Position
            input.Changed:Connect(function() if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then dragging = false end end)
        end
    end)
    TopBar.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then dragInput = input end
    end)
    UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input == dragInput and dragging then
            local delta = input.Position - dragStart
            MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
        end
    end)

    local Line = Instance.new("Frame")
    Line.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 1)
    Line.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 50)
    Line.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 45)
    Line.BorderSizePixel = 0
    Line.Parent = MainFrame

    local VLine = Instance.new("Frame")
    VLine.Size = UDim2.new(0, 1, 1, -50)
    VLine.Position = UDim2.new(0, 180, 0, 50)
    VLine.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 45)
    VLine.BorderSizePixel = 0
    VLine.Parent = MainFrame

    local Sidebar = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
    Sidebar.Size = UDim2.new(0, 175, 1, -50)
    Sidebar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 50)
    Sidebar.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    Sidebar.BorderSizePixel = 0
    Sidebar.ScrollBarThickness = 0
    Sidebar.Parent = MainFrame

    local SidebarLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    SidebarLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
    SidebarLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
    SidebarLayout.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center
    SidebarLayout.Parent = Sidebar
    Instance.new("UIPadding", Sidebar).PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 15)

    local sidebarOrder = 0
    local function NextSidebarOrder()
        sidebarOrder = sidebarOrder + 1
        return sidebarOrder
    end

    local ContentContainer = Instance.new("Frame")
    ContentContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, -180, 1, -50)
    ContentContainer.Position = UDim2.new(0, 180, 0, 50)
    ContentContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    ContentContainer.Parent = MainFrame

    local Window = { CurrentTab = nil, AllTabs = {} }

    function Window:MakeTabSection(name)
        local Sec = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Sec.Size = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0, 25)
        Sec.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Sec.Text = string.upper(name)
        Sec.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 120, 120)
        Sec.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Sec.TextSize = 11
        Sec.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Sec.LayoutOrder = NextSidebarOrder()
        Sec.Parent = Sidebar
        Instance.new("UIPadding", Sec).PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 5)
    end

    function Window:MakeTab(tabName, iconId)
        local TabBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        TabBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 155, 0, 40)
        TabBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        TabBtn.Text = ""
        TabBtn.LayoutOrder = NextSidebarOrder()
        TabBtn.Parent = Sidebar

        local TabBg = Instance.new("Frame")
        TabBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        TabBg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 28)
        TabBg.Parent = TabBtn
        Instance.new("UICorner", TabBg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

        local Gradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
        Gradient.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.4, 1),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1)
        })
        Gradient.Parent = TabBg
        Gradient.Enabled = false

        local LeftIndicator = Instance.new("Frame")
        LeftIndicator.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.5, 0)
        LeftIndicator.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.25, 0)
        LeftIndicator.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
        LeftIndicator.Parent = TabBg
        LeftIndicator.Visible = false
        Instance.new("UICorner", LeftIndicator).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

        local textOffsetX = 15
        if iconId then
            local Icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
            Icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
            Icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -9)
            Icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            Icon.Image = iconId
            Icon.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            Icon.Parent = TabBg
            textOffsetX = 40
        end

        local TabText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        TabText.Size = UDim2.new(1, -textOffsetX, 1, 0)
        TabText.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0, 0)
        TabText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        TabText.Text = tabName
        TabText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
        TabText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
        TabText.TextSize = 13
        TabText.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        TabText.Parent = TabBg

        local TabContent = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
        TabContent.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        TabContent.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        TabContent.ScrollBarThickness = 3
        TabContent.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
        TabContent.Visible = false
        TabContent.Parent = ContentContainer

        local ContentLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
        ContentLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 10)
        ContentLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
        ContentLayout.Parent = TabContent

        local ContentPadding = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        ContentPadding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 20); ContentPadding.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 20)
        ContentPadding.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 15); ContentPadding.PaddingBottom = UDim.new(0, 20)
        ContentPadding.Parent = TabContent

        ContentLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(function()
            TabContent.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, ContentLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 30)
        end)

        table.insert(Window.AllTabs, {Btn = TabBtn, Bg = TabBg, Text = TabText, Grad = Gradient, Content = TabContent, Indicator = LeftIndicator})

        local function SelectTab()
            for _, t in ipairs(Window.AllTabs) do
                t.Content.Visible = false
                t.Grad.Enabled = false
                t.Indicator.Visible = false
                TweenService:Create(t.Bg, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 28)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(t.Text, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)}):Play()
                if t.Bg:FindFirstChildOfClass("ImageLabel") then
                    TweenService:Create(t.Bg:FindFirstChildOfClass("ImageLabel"), TweenInfo.new(0.2), {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)}):Play()
                end
            end
            TabContent.Visible = true
            Gradient.Enabled = true
            LeftIndicator.Visible = true
            TweenService:Create(TabBg, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 80, 160)}):Play()
            TweenService:Create(TabText, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
            if TabBg:FindFirstChildOfClass("ImageLabel") then
                TweenService:Create(TabBg:FindFirstChildOfClass("ImageLabel"), TweenInfo.new(0.2), {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
            end
        end

        TabBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(SelectTab)

        if not Window.CurrentTab then Window.CurrentTab = TabContent; SelectTab() end

        local Elements = {}
        local currentRow = nil
        local itemsInRow = 0

        local function GetParentFrame(isHalf)
            if not isHalf then currentRow = nil; itemsInRow = 0; return TabContent end
            if not currentRow or itemsInRow >= 2 then
                currentRow = Instance.new("Frame")
                currentRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 65) 
                currentRow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                currentRow.Parent = TabContent
                local RowLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
                RowLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
                RowLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 15)
                RowLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
                RowLayout.Parent = currentRow
                itemsInRow = 0
            end
            itemsInRow = itemsInRow + 1
            return currentRow
        end

        local function CreateIconBox(parent, iconId)
            local IconBg = Instance.new("Frame")
            IconBg.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 36)
            IconBg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0.5, -18)
            IconBg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 40)
            IconBg.Parent = parent
            Instance.new("UICorner", IconBg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            Instance.new("UIStroke", IconBg).Color = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 70) 

            local Icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
            Icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22)
            Icon.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -11, 0.5, -11)
            Icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            Icon.Image = iconId
            Icon.Parent = IconBg
            return 65 
        end

        function Elements:AddContentSection(name)
            GetParentFrame(false) 
            local Sec = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            Sec.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 35)
            Sec.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            Sec.Text = name
            Sec.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
            Sec.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            Sec.TextSize = 16
            Sec.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            Sec.Parent = TabContent
            
            local Line = Instance.new("Frame")
            Line.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 1)
            Line.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, -5)
            Line.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 45)
            Line.BorderSizePixel = 0
            Line.Parent = Sec
        end


        function Elements:AddParagraph(title, desc)
            GetParentFrame(false)
            local PFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
            PFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 55)
            PFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 24, 28)
            PFrame.Parent = TabContent
            Instance.new("UICorner", PFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            Instance.new("UIStroke", PFrame).Color = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 50)
            local TLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            TLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 20)
            TLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 8)
            TLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            TLabel.Text = title or ""
            TLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
            TLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            TLabel.TextSize = 12
            TLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            TLabel.Parent = PFrame
            local DLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            DLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 20)
            DLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 30)
            DLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            DLabel.Text = desc or ""
            DLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(130, 130, 130)
            DLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            DLabel.TextSize = 11
            DLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            DLabel.Parent = PFrame
            local Obj = {}
            function Obj:SetDesc(text) DLabel.Text = tostring(text) end
            return Obj
        end

        function Elements:AddBanner(title, desc, imageId, link)
            GetParentFrame(false) 
            
            local BannerFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
            BannerFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -5, 0, 140)
            BannerFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 24, 28)
            BannerFrame.ClipsDescendants = true 
            BannerFrame.Parent = TabContent
            
            Instance.new("UICorner", BannerFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            Instance.new("UIStroke", BannerFrame).Color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 55) 

            local BannerImage = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
            BannerImage.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 80)
            BannerImage.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
            BannerImage.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 35)
            BannerImage.Image = imageId
            BannerImage.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Crop
            BannerImage.Parent = BannerFrame

            local InfoFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
            InfoFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 60)
            InfoFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 80)
            InfoFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            InfoFrame.Parent = BannerFrame

            local TitleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            TitleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -120, 0, 20)
            TitleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 10)
            TitleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            TitleLabel.Text = title
            TitleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            TitleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            TitleLabel.TextSize = 14
            TitleLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            TitleLabel.Parent = InfoFrame

            local DescLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            DescLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -120, 0, 15)
            DescLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 30)
            DescLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            DescLabel.Text = desc
            DescLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            DescLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            DescLabel.TextSize = 11
            DescLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            DescLabel.Parent = InfoFrame

            local JoinBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
            JoinBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, 32)
            JoinBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -105, 0.5, -16)
            JoinBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(10, 190, 60)
            JoinBtn.Text = "Join"
            JoinBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            JoinBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            JoinBtn.TextSize = 13
            JoinBtn.Parent = InfoFrame
            Instance.new("UICorner", JoinBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
            
            JoinBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if setclipboard then
                    setclipboard(link)
                    JoinBtn.Text = "Copied!"
                    JoinBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 140, 40)
                    task.wait(1.5)
                    JoinBtn.Text = "Join"
                    JoinBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(10, 190, 60)
                else
                 warn("Executor không hỗ trợ setclipboard!")
                end
            end)
        end

        function Elements:AddToggle(name, iconId, default, isHalf, callback)
            local state = default or false
            local parentFrame = GetParentFrame(isHalf)

            local COLOR_ON_BG     = Color3.fromRGB(13, 30, 60)
            local COLOR_OFF_BG    = Color3.fromRGB(24, 24, 28)
            local COLOR_ON_STROKE = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
            local COLOR_OFF_STROKE= Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 50)
            local COLOR_ON_ICON   = Color3.fromRGB(20, 60, 130)
            local COLOR_OFF_ICON  = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 40)
            local COLOR_ON_SWITCH = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
            local COLOR_OFF_SWITCH= Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 55)

            local TglFrame = Instance.new("TextButton")
            TglFrame.Size = isHalf and UDim2.new(0.5, -7, 0, 65) or UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 65)
            TglFrame.BackgroundColor3 = state and COLOR_ON_BG or COLOR_OFF_BG
            TglFrame.Text = ""
            TglFrame.AutoButtonColor = false
            TglFrame.Parent = parentFrame
            Instance.new("UICorner", TglFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)

            local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
            Stroke.Color = state and COLOR_ON_STROKE or COLOR_OFF_STROKE
            Stroke.Thickness = state and 1.5 or 1
            Stroke.Parent = TglFrame

            local IconBg = nil
            local IconImg = nil
            local IconStroke = nil
            local textOffsetX = 15
            if iconId and iconId ~= "" then
                IconBg = Instance.new("Frame")
                IconBg.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 36)
                IconBg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0.5, -18)
                IconBg.BackgroundColor3 = state and COLOR_ON_ICON or COLOR_OFF_ICON
                IconBg.Parent = TglFrame
                Instance.new("UICorner", IconBg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
                IconStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
                IconStroke.Color = state and COLOR_ON_STROKE or Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 70)
                IconStroke.Parent = IconBg
                IconImg = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
                IconImg.Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22)
                IconImg.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -11, 0.5, -11)
                IconImg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                IconImg.Image = iconId
                IconImg.ImageColor3 = state and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(180, 180, 180)
                IconImg.Parent = IconBg
                textOffsetX = 65
            end

            local TitleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            TitleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -textOffsetX - 60, 0, 20)
            TitleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0.5, -15)
            TitleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            TitleLabel.Text = name
            TitleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            TitleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
            TitleLabel.TextSize = 13
            TitleLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            TitleLabel.Parent = TglFrame

            local SubLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            SubLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -textOffsetX - 60, 0, 15)
            SubLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0.5, 5)
            SubLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            SubLabel.Text = state and "ACTIVE" or "DISABLE"
            SubLabel.TextColor3 = state and COLOR_ON_STROKE or Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 100)
            SubLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            SubLabel.TextSize = 11
            SubLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            SubLabel.Parent = TglFrame

            local Indicator = Instance.new("Frame")
            Indicator.Size = UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 22)
            Indicator.Position = UDim2.new(1, -55, 0.5, -11)
            Indicator.BackgroundColor3 = state and COLOR_ON_SWITCH or COLOR_OFF_SWITCH
            Indicator.Parent = TglFrame
            Instance.new("UICorner", Indicator).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

            local Circle = Instance.new("Frame")
            Circle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
            Circle.Position = state and UDim2.new(1, -20, 0.5, -9) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -9)
            Circle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            Circle.Parent = Indicator
            Instance.new("UICorner", Circle).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

            local function UpdateVisuals(on, dur)
                local t = TweenInfo.new(dur or 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint)
                TweenService:Create(TglFrame,  t, {BackgroundColor3 = on and COLOR_ON_BG or COLOR_OFF_BG}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(Stroke,    t, {Color = on and COLOR_ON_STROKE or COLOR_OFF_STROKE, Thickness = on and 1.5 or 1}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(Indicator, t, {BackgroundColor3 = on and COLOR_ON_SWITCH or COLOR_OFF_SWITCH}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(Circle,    t, {Position = on and UDim2.new(1, -20, 0.5, -9) or UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.5, -9)}):Play()
                SubLabel.Text = on and "ACTIVE" or "DISABLE"
                TweenService:Create(SubLabel, t, {TextColor3 = on and COLOR_ON_STROKE or Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 100)}):Play()
                if IconBg then
                    TweenService:Create(IconBg, t, {BackgroundColor3 = on and COLOR_ON_ICON or COLOR_OFF_ICON}):Play()
                end
                if IconStroke then
                    TweenService:Create(IconStroke, t, {Color = on and COLOR_ON_STROKE or Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 70)}):Play()
                end
                if IconImg then
                    TweenService:Create(IconImg, t, {ImageColor3 = on and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(180, 180, 180)}):Play()
                end
            end

            TglFrame.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                state = not state
                UpdateVisuals(state, 0.3)
                callback(state)
            end)
        end

        function Elements:AddButton(name, iconId, isHalf, callback, subtitle)
            local parentFrame = GetParentFrame(isHalf)
            local Btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
            Btn.Size = isHalf and UDim2.new(0.5, -7, 0, 65) or UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 65)
            Btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 24, 28)
            Btn.Text = ""
            Btn.AutoButtonColor = false
            Btn.Parent = parentFrame
            Instance.new("UICorner", Btn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            local BtnStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
            BtnStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 50)
            BtnStroke.Parent = Btn

            -- Icon box (dùng lại CreateIconBox nhưng lưu ref để đổi màu khi hover)
            local IconBg = nil
            local IconImg = nil
            local textOffsetX = 15
            if iconId and iconId ~= "" then
                IconBg = Instance.new("Frame")
                IconBg.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 36)
                IconBg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0.5, -18)
                IconBg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 40)
                IconBg.Parent = Btn
                Instance.new("UICorner", IconBg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
                Instance.new("UIStroke", IconBg).Color = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 70)
                IconImg = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
                IconImg.Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 0, 22)
                IconImg.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -11, 0.5, -11)
                IconImg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                IconImg.Image = iconId
                IconImg.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 180, 180)
                IconImg.Parent = IconBg
                textOffsetX = 65
            end

            -- Arrow icon bên phải
            local ArrowIcon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
            ArrowIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
            ArrowIcon.Position = UDim2.new(1, -32, 0.5, -9)
            ArrowIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            ArrowIcon.Image = "rbxassetid://11293977931"
            ArrowIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(90, 90, 95)
            ArrowIcon.Parent = Btn

            local TitleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            TitleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            TitleLabel.Text = name
            TitleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            TitleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
            TitleLabel.TextSize = 13
            TitleLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

            if subtitle and subtitle ~= "" then
                TitleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -textOffsetX - 44, 0, 20)
                TitleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0.5, -15)
                TitleLabel.Parent = Btn
                local SubLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                SubLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -textOffsetX - 44, 0, 15)
                SubLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0.5, 5)
                SubLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                SubLabel.Text = subtitle
                SubLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(110, 110, 115)
                SubLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
                SubLabel.TextSize = 11
                SubLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                SubLabel.Parent = Btn
            else
                TitleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -textOffsetX - 44, 1, 0)
                TitleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0, 0)
                TitleLabel.Parent = Btn
            end

            local t_fast = TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint)
            local t_slow = TweenInfo.new(0.2,  Enum.EasingStyle.Quint)

            Btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(Btn,       t_slow, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 36)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(BtnStroke, t_slow, {Color = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 75)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(ArrowIcon, t_slow, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)}):Play()
                if IconBg  then TweenService:Create(IconBg,  t_slow, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 50, 90)}):Play() end
                if IconImg then TweenService:Create(IconImg, t_slow, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play() end
            end)
            Btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(Btn,       t_slow, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 24, 28)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(BtnStroke, t_slow, {Color = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 50)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(ArrowIcon, t_slow, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(90, 90, 95)}):Play()
                if IconBg  then TweenService:Create(IconBg,  t_slow, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 40)}):Play() end
                if IconImg then TweenService:Create(IconImg, t_slow, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 180, 180)}):Play() end
            end)
            Btn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(Btn,       t_fast, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 40, 80)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(BtnStroke, t_fast, {Color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)}):Play()
            end)
            Btn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(Btn,       t_fast, {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 36)}):Play()
                TweenService:Create(BtnStroke, t_fast, {Color = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 75)}):Play()
            end)
            Btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(callback)
        end

        function Elements:AddDropdown(name, options, isHalf, callback)
            local isDropped = false
            local parentFrame = GetParentFrame(isHalf)
            local currentSelected = options and options[1] or "Trống"
            
            local DropBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
            DropBtn.Size = isHalf and UDim2.new(0.5, -7, 0, 65) or UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 65)
            DropBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 24, 28)
            DropBtn.Text = ""
            DropBtn.Parent = parentFrame
            Instance.new("UICorner", DropBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            Instance.new("UIStroke", DropBtn).Color = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 50)

            local textOffsetX = CreateIconBox(DropBtn, "rbxassetid://10734963191") 
            
            local TitleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            TitleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -textOffsetX, 0, 20)
            TitleLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0.5, -15)
            TitleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            TitleLabel.Text = name
            TitleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            TitleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
            TitleLabel.TextSize = 13
            TitleLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            TitleLabel.Parent = DropBtn

            local SelectedLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            SelectedLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -textOffsetX, 0, 15)
            SelectedLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, textOffsetX, 0.5, 5)
            SelectedLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            SelectedLabel.Text = "Select: " .. currentSelected
            SelectedLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            SelectedLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
            SelectedLabel.TextSize = 11
            SelectedLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            SelectedLabel.Parent = DropBtn

            local Arrow = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            Arrow.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
            Arrow.Position = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0.5, -10)
            Arrow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            Arrow.Text = "▼"
            Arrow.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            Arrow.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            Arrow.TextSize = 12
            Arrow.Parent = DropBtn

            local PopupFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
            PopupFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(32, 32, 36)
            PopupFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
            PopupFrame.Visible = false
            PopupFrame.ZIndex = 100 
            PopupFrame.ClipsDescendants = true
            PopupFrame.Parent = MainFrame 
            Instance.new("UICorner", PopupFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
            Instance.new("UIStroke", PopupFrame).Color = Color3.fromRGB(60, 60, 65)

            local ItemContainer = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
            ItemContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, -10)
            ItemContainer.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 5)
            ItemContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            ItemContainer.ScrollBarThickness = 2
            ItemContainer.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)
            ItemContainer.ZIndex = 101
            ItemContainer.Parent = PopupFrame

            local ItemLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
            ItemLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
            ItemLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
            ItemLayout.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center
            ItemLayout.Parent = ItemContainer

            TabContent:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CanvasPosition"):Connect(function()
                if isDropped then
                    isDropped = false
                    TweenService:Create(PopupFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {Size = UDim2.new(0, DropBtn.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 0)}):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(Arrow, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {Rotation = 0}):Play()
                    task.delay(0.2, function() if not isDropped then PopupFrame.Visible = false end end)
                end
            end)

            DropBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                isDropped = not isDropped
                if isDropped then
                    local relX = DropBtn.AbsolutePosition.X - MainFrame.AbsolutePosition.X
                    local relY = DropBtn.AbsolutePosition.Y - MainFrame.AbsolutePosition.Y
                    PopupFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, relX, 0, relY + DropBtn.AbsoluteSize.Y + 5)
                    PopupFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, DropBtn.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 0)
                    PopupFrame.Visible = true

                    local targetHeight = math.clamp(#options * 32, 0, 150) + 10
                    TweenService:Create(PopupFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint), {Size = UDim2.new(0, DropBtn.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, targetHeight)}):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(Arrow, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {Rotation = 180}):Play()
                else
                    TweenService:Create(PopupFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {Size = UDim2.new(0, DropBtn.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 0)}):Play()
                    TweenService:Create(Arrow, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {Rotation = 0}):Play()
                    task.delay(0.2, function() if not isDropped then PopupFrame.Visible = false end end)
                end
            end)

            local Funcs = {}
            function Funcs:Refresh(newOptions)
                options = newOptions
                for _, child in pairs(ItemContainer:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("TextButton") then child:Destroy() end end

                for _, opt in ipairs(options) do
                    local OptBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                    OptBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 28)
                    OptBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 45)
                    OptBtn.Text = "   " .. opt
                    OptBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
                    OptBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
                    OptBtn.TextSize = 12
                    OptBtn.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                    OptBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
                    OptBtn.ZIndex = 102
                    OptBtn.Parent = ItemContainer
                    Instance.new("UICorner", OptBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

                    OptBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function() TweenService:Create(OptBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 55), TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 130, 246)}):Play() end)
                    OptBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function() TweenService:Create(OptBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.15), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 45), TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)}):Play() end)

                    OptBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                        SelectedLabel.Text = "Select: " .. opt
                        isDropped = false
                        TweenService:Create(PopupFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {Size = UDim2.new(0, DropBtn.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 0)}):Play()
                        TweenService:Create(Arrow, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {Rotation = 0}):Play()
                        task.delay(0.2, function() if not isDropped then PopupFrame.Visible = false end end)
                        callback(opt)
                    end)
                end
                ItemContainer.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, ItemLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 5)
            end

            Funcs:Refresh(options)
            return Funcs
        end

        return Elements
    end
    return Window
end
-- ===== DELTA X COMPATIBILITY SHIMS =====
-- Ensure hookfunction works on Delta X (uses hookfunc alias)
if not hookfunction and hookfunc then
    hookfunction = hookfunc
elseif not hookfunction then
    hookfunction = function(f, r) return r end -- no-op fallback
end
-- Ensure newcclosure works
if not newcclosure then
    newcclosure = function(f) return f end
end
-- Ensure getnamecallmethod works
if not getnamecallmethod then
    getnamecallmethod = function() return "" end
end
-- ========================================

local Services = setmetatable({}, {
    __index = function(self, serviceName)
        local service = game:GetService(serviceName)
        rawset(self, serviceName, service)
        return service
    end
})

local function NotificacaoNightMystic(titulo, mensagem)
    local success = pcall(function()
        local TweenService = Services.TweenService
        local CoreGui = Services.CoreGui
        local LogoID = "rbxassetid://89906421818860"

        local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        ScreenGui.Name = "NM_Notify"
        ScreenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
        ScreenGui.Parent = CoreGui
        
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Parent = ScreenGui
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(8, 8, 8)
        Frame.Position = UDim2.new(1, 20, 0.85, 0)
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 280, 0, 65)
        Frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        
        local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        UICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
        UICorner.Parent = Frame
        
        local UIStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        UIStroke.Parent = Frame
        UIStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45)
        UIStroke.Thickness = 1

        local Logo = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
        Logo.Parent = Frame
        Logo.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Logo.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
        Logo.Size = UDim2.new(0, 45, 0, 45)
        Logo.Image = LogoID
        Logo.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit

        local Title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Title.Parent = Frame
        Title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Title.Position = UDim2.new(0, 65, 0, 12)
        Title.Size = UDim2.new(1, -70, 0, 20)
        Title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Title.Text = titulo
        Title.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        Title.TextSize = 14
        Title.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Title.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd

        local Msg = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Msg.Parent = Frame
        Msg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Msg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 65, 0, 32)
        Msg.Size = UDim2.new(1, -70, 0, 20)
        Msg.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Msg.Text = mensagem
        Msg.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        Msg.TextSize = 12
        Msg.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Msg.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        
        local tweenIn = TweenService:Create(
            Frame, 
            TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),
            {Position = UDim2.new(1, -300, 0.85, 0)}
        )
        tweenIn:Play()

        task.delay(10, function()
            if Frame and Frame.Parent then
                local tweenOut = TweenService:Create(
                    Frame,
                    TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In),
                    {Position = UDim2.new(1, 20, 0.85, 0)}
                )
                tweenOut:Play()
                tweenOut.Completed:Wait()
                ScreenGui:Destroy()
            end
        end)
    end)
    
    if not success then
        warn("[Moonlight Hub] Error notification")
    end
end

NotificacaoNightMystic("Moonlight Hub", "script has loaded successfully!")

-- ========================================
-- SAVE SYSTEM (Optimized)
-- ========================================
local HttpService = Services.HttpService
local FolderName = "Moonlight Hub Hub"
local FileName = "Settings.json"
local FullPath = FolderName .. "/" .. FileName

if makefolder and not isfolder(FolderName) then 
    makefolder(FolderName) 
end

_G.SaveData = _G.SaveData or {}

function SaveSettings()
    if not writefile then return false end
    local success = pcall(function()
        local json = HttpService:JSONEncode(_G.SaveData)
        writefile(FullPath, json)
    end)
    return success
end

function LoadSettings()
    if not (isfile and isfile(FullPath)) then return false end
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        local content = readfile(FullPath)
        return HttpService:JSONDecode(content)
    end)
    if success and result then 
        _G.SaveData = result
        return true
    end
    return false
end

function GetSetting(name, default)
    return _G.SaveData[name] ~= nil and _G.SaveData[name] or default
end

LoadSettings()

-- ========================================
-- AUTO KEN (Observation Haki)
-- ========================================
local Players = Services.Players
local CollectionService = Services.CollectionService
local ReplicatedStorage = Services.ReplicatedStorage

local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local commE = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("CommE")

_G.AutoKen = true

local function HasKen()
    local char = player.Character
    return char and CollectionService:HasTag(char, "Ken")
end

task.spawn(function()
    while _G.AutoKen do
        task.wait(0.2)
        if not HasKen() then
            pcall(function()
                commE:FireServer("Ken", true)
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- ========================================
-- AUTO TEAM & LIGHTING
-- ========================================
local desiredTeam = "Marines"

if not player.Team or player.Team.Name ~= desiredTeam then
    pcall(function()
        ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("SetTeam", desiredTeam)
    end)
end

local Lighting = Services.Lighting

-- Full bright (optimized lighting)
Lighting.Ambient = Color3.new(0.695, 0.695, 0.695)
Lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = Color3.new(0.695, 0.695, 0.695)
Lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.new(0.695, 0.695, 0.695)
Lighting.Brightness = 2
Lighting.FogEnd = 1e10

-- ========================================
-- GLOBAL VARIABLES (Cached & Organized)
-- ========================================
do
    ply = Services.Players

EquipWeapon = function(I)
		if not I then
			return;
		end;
		if plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(I) then
			plr.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(I));
		end;
	end;
weaponSc = function(I)
		for e, K in pairs(plr.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
			if K:IsA("Tool") then
				if K.ToolTip == I then
					EquipWeapon(K.Name);
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
-- Delta X compatible hookfunction wrapper
local _hookfn = hookfunction or hookfunc or (function(f, r) return r end)
pcall(function()
    _hookfn(require((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Effect.Container.Death), function() end)
end)
pcall(function()
    _hookfn((require((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):WaitForChild("GuideModule"))).ChangeDisplayedNPC, function() end)
end)
pcall(function()
    _hookfn(error, function() end)
end)
pcall(function()
    _hookfn(warn, function() end)
end)

local G = {};
G.__index = G;
G.Alive = function(I)
		if not I then
			return;
		end;
		local e = I:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
		return e and e.Health > 0;
	end;
G.Pos = function(I, e)
		local target = PosMon and (typeof(PosMon) == "CFrame" and PosMon.Position or PosMon) or Root.Position
		return (Root.Position - target).Magnitude <= e
	end;
G.Dist = function(I, e)
		return (Root.Position - (I:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")).Position).Magnitude <= e;
	end;
G.DistH = function(I, e)
		return (Root.Position - (I:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")).Position).Magnitude > e;
	end;
-- ALTURA ÚNICA AJUSTÁVEL DO MOB
_G.MobHeight = _G.MobHeight or 20

G.Kill = function(I, e)
	if not (I and e) then return end

	local hrp = I:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if not hrp then return end

	-- trava posição do mob
	if not I:GetAttribute("Locked") then
		I:SetAttribute("Locked", hrp.CFrame)
	end

	-- posição alvo do bring
	PosMon = (I:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position

	-- >>> FORÇA O BRING <<<
	_B = true
	BringEnemy()

	-- equipa arma
	EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)

	local tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
	if not tool then return end

	-- TP acima do mob (altura única)
	_tp(hrp.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, _G.MobHeight, 0))
end
G.Kill2 = function(I, e)
		if I and e then
			if not I:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				I:SetAttribute("Locked", I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (I:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon);
			local e = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
			local K = e.ToolTip;
			if K == "Blox Fruit" then
				_tp((I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0));
			else
				_tp((I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 8)) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0));
			end;
			if RandomCFrame then
				wait(.1);
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(25, 30, 0));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
G.KillSea = function(I, e)
		if I and e then
			if not I:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				I:SetAttribute("Locked", I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;

	end;

_G.FruitSkills = {
    Z = false,
    X = false,
    C = false,
    V = false,
    F = false
}

UseFruitSkills = function()
    weaponSc("Blox Fruit")

    if _G.FruitSkills.Z then
        Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z")
    end
    if _G.FruitSkills.X then
        Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X")
    end
    if _G.FruitSkills.C then
        Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C")
    end
    if _G.FruitSkills.V then
        Useskills("Blox Fruit", "V")
    end
    if _G.FruitSkills.F then
        vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "F", false, game)
        vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "F", false, game)
    end
end

G.Mas = function(I, e)
		if I and e then
			if not I:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				I:SetAttribute("Locked", I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (I:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			if I.Humanoid.Health <= HealthM then
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0));
				UseFruitSkills()
			else
				weaponSc("Melee");
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
G.Masgun = function(I, e)
		if I and e then
			if not I:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				I:SetAttribute("Locked", I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (I:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			if I.Humanoid.Health <= HealthM then
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 35, 8));
				Useskills("Gun", "Z");
				Useskills("Gun", "X");
			else
				weaponSc("Melee");
				_tp(I.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;

		if I == "Melee" then

				replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Demon Fruit", e);
			end;
		end;

    Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,

-- FUNÇÃO: VERIFICA SE QUALQUER FARM ESTÁ ATIVO

local function FarmAtivo()
    -- PRIORIDADE ABSOLUTA (ELF)
    if _G.FarmPriorityElf or _G.FarmElfLevelCustom then
        return true
    end

    -- AUTO MASTERY ALL SWORD (INDEPENDENTE DO START FARM)  
    if _G.FarmMastery_S then  
        return true  
    end  

    -- OUTROS FARMS (DEPENDENTES DO START FARM)  
    return _G.StartFarm and (
        _G.Level or  
        _G.AutoFarm_Bone or  
        _G.AutoFarm_Cake or  
        _G.FarmMastery_Dev or  
        _G.FarmMastery_G or

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÃO: IGNORA MOBS INDESEJADOS
--==================================================
local function IsRaidMob(mob)
    local n = mob.Name:lower()

    if n:find("raid") or n:find("microchip") or n:find("island") then  
        return true  
    end  

    if mob:GetAttribute("IsRaid")  
        or mob:GetAttribute("RaidMob")  
        or mob:GetAttribute("IsBoss") then  
        return true  
    end  

    local hum = mob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")  
    if hum and hum.WalkSpeed == 0 then  
        return true  
    end  

    if mob.Parent and tostring(mob.Parent):lower():find("_worldorigin") then  
        return true  
    end  

    return false
end

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÃO PRINCIPAL: BRING
--==================================================
BringEnemy = function()
    if not FarmAtivo() or not _B then return end

    local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer  
    local char = plr.Character  
    local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")  
    if not hrp then return end  

    -- Simulation Radius  
    pcall(function()  
        sethiddenproperty(plr, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)  
    end)  

    local targetPos = PosMon and (typeof(PosMon) == "CFrame" and PosMon.Position or PosMon) or hrp.Position
    local enemies = workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()  
    local count = 0  

    for _, mob in ipairs(enemies) do  
        if count >= _G.MaxBringMobs then break end  

        local hum = mob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")  
        local root = mob:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")  

        if hum and root and hum.Health > 0 and not IsRaidMob(mob) then  
            local dist = (root.Position - targetPos).Magnitude  

            if dist > 5 and dist <= _G.BringRange and not root:GetAttribute("Tweening") then
                count += 1  
                root:SetAttribute("Tweening", true)  

                local tween = TweenService:Create(  
                    root,  
                    TweenInfoBring,  
                    { CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos) }  
                )  

                tween:Play()  
                tween.Completed:Once(function()  
                    if root then  
                        root:SetAttribute("Tweening", false)  
                    end  
                end)  
            end  
        end  
    end
end

--==================================================
-- LOOP CONTROLADOR
--==================================================
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.5) do
        if FarmAtivo() then
            _B = true
            BringEnemy()
        else
            _B = false
        end
    end
end)
Useskills = function(I, e)
		if I == "Melee" then
			weaponSc("Melee");
			if e == "Z" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "Z", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "Z", false, game);
			elseif e == "X" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "X", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "X", false, game);
			elseif e == "C" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "C", false, game);

						e[2] = MousePos;

				end;
			end;
		end;

GetConnectionEnemies = function(I)
		for e, K in pairs(replicated:GetChildren()) do
			if K:IsA("Model") and ((typeof(I) == "table" and table.find(I, K.Name) or K.Name == I) and (K:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and K.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
				return K;
			end;
		end;
		for e, K in next, game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren() do
			if K:IsA("Model") and ((typeof(I) == "table" and table.find(I, K.Name) or K.Name == I) and (K:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and K.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
				return K;
			end;
		end;
	end;
LowCpu = function()
		local I = true;
		local e = game;
		local K = e.Workspace;
		local n = e.Lighting;
		local d = K.Terrain;
		d.WaterWaveSize = 0;
		d.WaterWaveSpeed = 0;
		d.WaterReflectance = 0;
		d.WaterTransparency = 0;
		n.GlobalShadows = false;
		n.FogEnd = 9000000000.0;
		n.Brightness = 1;
		(settings()).Rendering.QualityLevel = "Level01";
		for e, K in pairs(e:GetDescendants()) do
			if K:IsA("Part") or K:IsA("Union") or K:IsA("CornerWedgePart") or K:IsA("TrussPart") then
				K.Material = "Plastic";
				K.Reflectance = 0;
			elseif K:IsA("Decal") or K:IsA("Texture") and I then
				K.Transparency = 1;
			elseif K:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or K:IsA("Trail") then
				K.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0);
			elseif K:IsA("Explosion") then
				K.BlastPressure = 1;
				K.BlastRadius = 1;
			elseif K:IsA("Fire") or K:IsA("SpotLight") or K:IsA("Smoke") or K:IsA("Sparkles") then
				K.Enabled = false;
			elseif K:IsA("MeshPart") then
				K.Material = "Plastic";
				K.Reflectance = 0;
				K.TextureID = 10385902758728957;
			end;
		end;
		for I, e in pairs(n:GetChildren()) do
			if e:IsA("BlurEffect") or e:IsA("SunRaysEffect") or e:IsA("ColorCorrectionEffect") or e:IsA("BloomEffect") or e:IsA("DepthOfFieldEffect") then
				e.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	end;

		for I, e in next, plr.Backpack:GetChildren() do
			if string.find(e.Name, "Fruit") then
				EquipWeapon(e.Name);
				wait(.1);
				if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible == true then
					plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible = false;
				end;
				EquipWeapon(e.Name);
				(plr.Character:FindFirstChild(e.Name)).EatRemote:InvokeServer("Drop");
			end;
		end;
		for I, e in pairs(plr.Character:GetChildren()) do
			if string.find(e.Name, "Fruit") then
				EquipWeapon(e.Name);
				wait(.1);
				if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible == true then
					plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible = false;
				end;
				EquipWeapon(e.Name);
				(plr.Character:FindFirstChild(e.Name)).EatRemote:InvokeServer("Drop");
			end;
		end;
	end;

GetIn = function(I)
		for e, K in pairs(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
			if type(K) == "table" then
				if K.Name == I or plr.Character:FindFirstChild(I) or plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(I) then
					return true;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		return false;
	end;

		for e, K in pairs(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
			if type(K) == "table" then
				if K.Type == "Material" then
					if K.Name == I then
						return K.Count;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		return 0;
	end;

getInfinity_Ability = function(I, e)
		if not Root then
			return;
		end;
		if I == "Soru" and e then
			for I, K in next, getgc() do
				if plr.Character.Soru then
					if typeof(K) == "function" and (getfenv(K)).script == plr.Character.Soru then
						for I, K in next, getupvalues(K) do
							if typeof(K) == "table" then
								repeat
									wait(Sec);
									K.LastUse = 0;
								until not e or plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		elseif I == "Energy" and e then
			plr.Character.Energy.Changed:connect(function()
				if e then
					plr.Character.Energy.Value = Energy;
				end;
			end);
		elseif I == "Observation" and e then
			local I = plr.VisionRadius;
			I.Value = math.huge;
		end;
	end;

		pcall(function()

				for I, e in next, e do
					if tonumber(e.Count) < 12 then
						TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, I);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;

task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		if C and C.Parent == workspace then
			if shouldTween then
				(getgenv()).OnFarm = true;
			else
				(getgenv()).OnFarm = false;
			end;
		else
			(getgenv()).OnFarm = false;
		end;
	end;
end);

task.spawn(function()
	local I = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
	repeat task.wait() until I.Character and I.Character.PrimaryPart;

	C.CFrame = I.Character.PrimaryPart.CFrame;

	while task.wait() do
		pcall(function()
			if (getgenv()).OnFarm then
				if C and C.Parent == workspace then
					local e = I.Character and I.Character.PrimaryPart;
					if e and (e.Position - C.Position).Magnitude <= 200 then
						e.CFrame = C.CFrame;
					else
						C.CFrame = e.CFrame;
					end;
				end;

				local e = I.Character;
				if e then
					for _, v in pairs(e:GetChildren()) do
						if v:IsA("BasePart") then
							v.CanCollide = false;
						end;
					end;
				end;

			else
				local e = I.Character;
				if e then
					for _, v in pairs(e:GetChildren()) do
						if v:IsA("BasePart") then
							v.CanCollide = true;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

-- =======================
-- TWEEN AJUSTADO POR DISTÂNCIA
-- =======================

-- [[ VARIÁVEIS PARA O SEU INPUT ]] --
getgenv().TweenSpeedFar = 300   -- Velocidade Padrão (Longe)
getgenv().TweenSpeedNear = 600  -- Velocidade Boost (Perto <= 15 studs)

_tp = function(I)
local e = plr.Character;
if not e or not e:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
return;
end;

local HRP = e.HumanoidRootPart;  

-- Desativar farm enquanto tweena  
shouldTween = true  
getgenv().OnFarm = false  

-- Garantir que não está ancorado  
if HRP.Anchored then  
	HRP.Anchored = false  
	task.wait()  
end  

local dist = (I.Position - HRP.Position).Magnitude  

-- ===============================  
--  SE ESTIVER ATÉ 15 STUDS → USA A VELOCIDADE DE PERTO
--  CASO CONTRÁRIO → USA A VELOCIDADE PADRÃO
-- ===============================  
local speed = dist <= 15 and (getgenv().TweenSpeedNear or 600) or (getgenv().TweenSpeedFar or 300)

local info = TweenInfo.new(dist / speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)  
local tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(C, info, { CFrame = I })  

-- Caso esteja sentado  
if e.Humanoid.Sit == true then  
	C.CFrame = CFrame.new(C.Position.X, I.Y, C.Position.Z)  
end  

tween:Play()  

-- Anti travamento / controle  
task.spawn(function()  
	while tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do  
		if not shouldTween then  
			tween:Cancel()  
			break  
		end  
		task.wait(.1)  
	end  

	getgenv().OnFarm = true  
end)

end

TeleportToTarget = function(I)
_tp(I)
end

notween = function(I)
plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = I
end


function BTP(I)
	local e = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
	local K = e.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
	local n = e.Character.Humanoid;
	local d = e.PlayerGui.Main;
	local z = I.Position;
	local H = K.Position;

	repeat
		n.Health = 0;
		K.CFrame = I;
		d.Quest.Visible = false;

		if (K.Position - H).Magnitude > 1 then
			H = K.Position;
			K.CFrame = I;
		end;

		task.wait(.5);
	until (I.Position - K.Position).Magnitude <= 2000;
end;

QuestBeta = function()
		local I = QuestB();
		return {
			[0] = _G.FindBoss,
			[1] = bMon,
			[2] = Qdata,
			[3] = Qname,
			[4] = PosB,
		};
	end;

--  HOP TABS (from MoonLightHub)
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PROXY: FastAttackModule (UI gọi ngay, logic load ngầm sau)
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
local _FA_active   = false
local _FA_setting  = {}
local _FA_cdaat    = 80
local _FA_timewait = 10
local _FA_real     = nil

local FastAttackModule = {}
function FastAttackModule:SetActive(s)   _FA_active = s;   if _FA_real then _FA_real:SetActive(s) end end
function FastAttackModule:InputSetting(t) _FA_setting = t; if _FA_real then _FA_real:InputSetting(t) end end
function FastAttackModule:InputValue(c,w) _FA_cdaat=c; _FA_timewait=w; if _FA_real then _FA_real:InputValue(c,w) end end

-- Load thật ngầm sau khi game ready
task.spawn(function()
    repeat task.wait(0.5) until game:IsLoaded()
    repeat task.wait(0.5) until game.Players.LocalPlayer
    repeat task.wait(0.5) until game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("PlayerScripts")

    local ok, CF = pcall(require, game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild("CombatFramework", 10))
    if not ok or not CF then return end

    local CFR = pcall(getupvalues, CF) and getupvalues(CF)[2] or nil
    if not CFR then return end

    local UFFF = false; local Count = 0; local TickC = tick()
    local settings_fa = {CDAAT=80, TimeWait=10}; local cfg = {}

    local function CurrentWeapon()
        local ac = CFR.activeController
        local ret = ac and ac.blades and ac.blades[1]
        if not ret then return pcall(function() return game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool").Name end) end
        pcall(function() while ret.Parent ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character do ret = ret.Parent end end)
        return ret
    end

    local function DoAttack()
        if not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character then return end
        local stunV = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Stun")
        if stunV and stunV.Value ~= 0 then return end
        local ac = CFR.activeController
        if not (ac and ac.equipped) then return end
        ac.hitboxMagnitude = 55
        local ok2, bladehit = pcall(function()
            return require(game.ReplicatedStorage.CombatFramework.RigLib).getBladeHits(
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character, {game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart}, 60)
        end)
        if not ok2 or #bladehit == 0 then return end
        local ok3 = pcall(function()
            local v5=debug.getupvalue(ac.attack,5); local v6=debug.getupvalue(ac.attack,6)
            local v4=debug.getupvalue(ac.attack,4); local v7=debug.getupvalue(ac.attack,7)
            local n12=(v5*798405+v4*727595)%v6; local n13=v4*798405
            n12=(n12*v6+n13)%1099511627776; v5=math.floor(n12/v6); v4=n12-v5*v6; v7=v7+1
            debug.setupvalue(ac.attack,5,v5); debug.setupvalue(ac.attack,6,v6)
            debug.setupvalue(ac.attack,4,v4); debug.setupvalue(ac.attack,7,v7)
            for _,v in pairs(ac.animator.anims.basic) do v:Play(0.01,0.01,0.01) end
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") and ac.blades and ac.blades[1] then
                game.ReplicatedStorage.RigControllerEvent:FireServer("weaponChange", tostring(CurrentWeapon()))
                game.ReplicatedStorage.RigControllerEvent:FireServer("hit", bladehit, 2, "")
            end
        end)
    end

    local R = {}
    function R:SetActive(s) UFFF=s end
    function R:InputSetting(t) cfg=t end
    function R:InputValue(c,w) settings_fa.CDAAT=c; settings_fa.TimeWait=w end
    function R:GetCount() return Count end
    function R:GetMethod() return Count < settings_fa.CDAAT and "Fast" or "Slow" end

    _FA_real = R
    R:SetActive(_FA_active); R:InputSetting(_FA_setting); R:InputValue(_FA_cdaat, _FA_timewait)

    -- Hook count
    pcall(function()
        local MT = getrawmetatable(game); local Old = MT.__namecall; setreadonly(MT,false)
        MT.__namecall = newcclosure(function(self,...)
            local m = getnamecallmethod(); local a = {...}
            if m=="FireServer" and self.Name=="RigControllerEvent" and a[1]=="hit" then Count=Count+1; TickC=tick() end
            return Old(self,unpack(a))
        end)
    end)

    -- Attack loop
    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait() do if UFFF then pcall(function()
            if cfg["Mastery Farm"] then pcall(DoAttack); task.wait(cfg.DelayAttack or 0.2)
            elseif Count < settings_fa.CDAAT then pcall(DoAttack)
            else pcall(DoAttack); task.wait((cfg.DelayAttack or 0.2)*2) end
        end) end end
    end)
    -- Controller loop
    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait() do if UFFF then pcall(function()
            local F = getupvalues(require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts.CombatFramework))[2]
            F.activeController.hitboxMagnitude=55; F.activeController.timeToNextAttack=0
            F.activeController.attacking=false; F.activeController.increment=3
            F.activeController.blocking=false; F.activeController.timeToNextBlock=0
            F.activeController:attack(); task.wait(0.2)
        end) end end
    end)
    -- Count reset loop
    task.spawn(function()
        while task.wait() do pcall(function()
            if tick()-TickC >= settings_fa.TimeWait then Count=0 end
        end) end
    end)
end)

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  HELPER GLOBALS (an toàn, không block)
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    return I and I:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and I.Humanoid.Health > 0
end

local HOP_APIS = {
    ["Sword Legend"]        = "http://nighthub.site/boss/SwordLegendary",
    ["Haki Legendary"]      = "http://nighthub.site/boss/HakiLegendary",
    ["Rip Indra"]           = "http://nighthub.site/boss/RipIndra",
    ["Darkbeard"]           = "http://nighthub.site/boss/Darkbeard",
    ["Dough King"]          = "http://nighthub.site/boss/DoughKing",
    ["Berry"]               = "http://nighthub.site/boss/Berry",
    ["Tyrant Of The Skies"] = "http://nighthub.site/boss/TyrantOfTheSkies",
    ["Cursed Captain"]      = "http://nighthub.site/boss/CursedCaptain",
    ["Soul Reaper"]         = "http://nighthub.site/boss/SoulReaper",
    ["Full Moon"]           = "http://nighthub.site/boss/Fullmoon",
    ["Near Moon"]           = "http://nighthub.site/boss/NearMoon",
    ["Mirage Island"]       = "http://nighthub.site/boss/Mirage",
    ["Kitsune Island"]      = "http://nighthub.site/boss/KitsuneIsland",
    ["Prehistoric Island"]  = "http://nighthub.site/boss/PrehistoricIsland",
    ["Cake Prince"]         = "http://nighthub.site/boss/CakePrince",
    ["Elite"]               = "http://nighthub.site/boss/Elite",
    ["Castle Raid"]         = "http://nighthub.site/boss/CastleRaid",
}

local function Notify(title, text)
    pcall(function() game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{Title=title,Text=text,Duration=3}) end)
end

local function FetchServers(apiKey)
    local url = HOP_APIS[apiKey]
    if not url then return {} end
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local reqFunc = (typeof(syn)=="table" and syn.request) or (typeof(request)=="function" and request) or http_request
        local res = reqFunc({Url=url, Method="GET"})
        return HttpSvc:JSONDecode(res.Body)
    end)
    return (ok and type(result)=="table") and result or {}
end

local function HopToServer(apiKey, onlyLow, maxPly)
    task.spawn(function()
        local servers = FetchServers(apiKey)
        if #servers == 0 then Notify("Hop","Không tìm thấy server!"); return end
        table.sort(servers, function(a,b) return (a.players or 99)<(b.players or 99) end)
        local target
        for _, s in ipairs(servers) do
            if not onlyLow or (s.players or 99) <= (maxPly or 12) then
                if tostring(s.jobId) ~= tostring(game.JobId) then target = s; break end
            end
        end
        if target and target.jobId then
            pcall(function() game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, target.jobId, plr) end)
        else
            Notify("Hop","Không có server phù hợp!")
        end
    end)
end

local function RejoinServer()
    pcall(function() game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, plr) end)
end

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  FARMING TAB
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  HOP TAB
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Window:MakeTabSection("Hop Tab")

-- Helper tạo section hop chuẩn
local function MakeHopSection(tab, apiKey, farmDef)
    local onlyLow = false
    local maxPly  = 8

    tab:AddContentSection("Server List")
    tab:AddButton("Click to Refresh List", "rbxassetid://10734886960", false, function()
        task.spawn(function()
            local s = FetchServers(apiKey)
            Notify("Hop", "Tìm thấy " .. #s .. " server!")
        end)
    end)

    tab:AddContentSection("Hop Options")
    tab:AddToggle("Auto Hop",               "rbxassetid://10709797382", false, true, function(s)
        _G["AutoHop_"..apiKey] = s
        if s then task.spawn(function()
            while _G["AutoHop_"..apiKey] do HopToServer(apiKey,onlyLow,maxPly); task.wait(5) end
        end) end
    end)
    tab:AddToggle("Only Low Player Server", "rbxassetid://10747373176", false, true, function(s) onlyLow=s end)
    tab:AddDropdown("Max Players", {"4","5","6","7","8","9","10","11","12"}, false, function(o) maxPly=tonumber(o) or 8 end)

    if farmDef then
        tab:AddContentSection("Auto Farm")
        tab:AddToggle(farmDef.name, farmDef.icon or "rbxassetid://10747363465", false, false, function(s)
            task.spawn(function() farmDef.callback(s) end)
        end)
    end

    tab:AddContentSection("Actions")
    tab:AddButton("Hop to Best Server",    "rbxassetid://10734961809", true, function() HopToServer(apiKey,onlyLow,maxPly) end)
    tab:AddButton("Rejoin Current Server", "rbxassetid://10734886960", true, function() RejoinServer() end)
end

-- ── CAKE PRINCE ───────────────────────────
local CakePrinceTab = Window:MakeTab("Cake Prince", "rbxassetid://10709783217")
MakeHopSection(CakePrinceTab, "Cake Prince", {
    name="Auto Farm Cake Prince", icon="rbxassetid://10747363465",
    callback=function(state)
        _G.AutoFarm_Cake=state; _G.StartFarm=state
        while state and _G.AutoFarm_Cake do task.wait()
            pcall(function()
                local hrp = plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then return end
                local E = workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies"); if not E then return end
                local CakePos = CFrame.new(-2091.91,70,-12142.83)
                local PortalEntrance = CFrame.new(-2151.82,149.32,-12404.91)
                local mirror = workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("CakeLoaf")
                local other = mirror and mirror:FindFirstChild("BigMirror") and mirror:FindFirstChild("BigMirror"):FindFirstChild("Other")
                local portalOpen = other and other.Transparency==0
                local boss = E:FindFirstChild("Cake Prince") or E:FindFirstChild("Dough King")
                if not boss and not portalOpen and (hrp.Position-CakePos.Position).Magnitude>3000 then _tp(CakePos); return end
                if boss and boss:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and boss.Humanoid.Health>0 and boss.PrimaryPart then
                    _tp(boss.PrimaryPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,25,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),0,0))
                    G.Kill(boss,true); return
                end
                if portalOpen then TeleportConditional(hrp,PortalEntrance,500); return end
                local MOBS={"Cookie Crafter","Cake Guard","Baking Staff","Head Baker"}
                local best,bd=nil,math.huge
                for _,m in ipairs(E:GetChildren()) do
                    if table.find(MOBS,m.Name) and G.Alive(m) then
                        local d=(m.HumanoidRootPart.Position-hrp.Position).Magnitude
                        if d<bd then bd=d; best=m end
                    end
                end
                if best then _tp(best.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,20,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),0,0)); G.Kill(best,true)
                else TeleportConditional(hrp,CFrame.new(-1927.92,37.80,-12842.54),TELEPORT_DISTANCE_THRESHOLD) end
            end)
        end
    end
})
